The only negative I have is about the food itself at the hotel buffet restaurant (the other restaurants were closed at the time so we only ate at the buffet in the lobby). msg:I went to Huzhou for a trip during the May Day holiday and stayed at the Sheraton Huzhou Hot Spring Resort Hotel (Moon Hotel), a landmark building of Taihu Lake. The hotel has a beautiful exterior and looks great when the lights are on, but the software inside is average, the facilities are old, and the service is not worth the high price. I booked a river view room, and the room price rose to more than 3,600 yuan during the May Day holiday. The room is not big, and the price-performance ratio is average. The advantages are rich breakfast categories, free travel photography, and free hot spring tickets (I didn't go on May 1st). It's okay to walk around and take pictures outside the hotel. At 18:00, the Moon Hotel lights up and there is a light show, which echoes the water show of the Rainbow Bridge. Taihu Ancient Town is 4 kilometers away. You can go for a walk at night. The night view is beautiful. There are light shows, water dance shows and fireworks shows on holidays, which are worth seeing.

Huzhou, this beautiful Jiangnan water town, always attracts tourists from all over the world with its unique charm. The Sheraton Hotel, located in its bustling area, has become the first choice for tourists with its high-quality service and superior geographical location. I recently had the honor of staying here and experienced its unique charm in person. Now I will share my feelings with you.

First of all, the geographical location of Huzhou Sheraton Hotel is very advantageous. It is located on the south bank of the scenic Taihu Lake, with a panoramic view of the lake and mountains. Every morning, when I open the window, the fresh air and the sparkling waves on the lake always make me happy. Moreover, the transportation around the hotel is very convenient, whether it is to the city or other attractions.

Secondly, the service quality of the hotel is impressive. From the moment I checked in, I felt the enthusiasm and thoughtfulness of the staff. They always smiled, patiently answered my various questions, and provided me with a lot of practical suggestions. The facilities in the guest room are also very complete, and the bed is comfortable and soft, so that I can have a good sleep every night. In addition, the hotel also provides a variety of dining options, whether it is the exquisite dishes of the Chinese restaurant or the exotic flavors of the Western restaurant, they can satisfy my taste buds.

I also spent a pleasant leisure time at the Sheraton Huzhou Hotel. The hotel's swimming pool and gym facilities are first-class, allowing me to maintain a healthy lifestyle during my trip. In addition, the hotel also provides a variety of entertainment activities, such as yoga classes, Tai Chi performances, etc., which made me feel relaxed and happy physically and mentally.

In general, the Sheraton Huzhou Hotel provides tourists with a perfect holiday experience with its superior geographical location, high-quality services and rich leisure facilities. If you plan to travel to Huzhou, you might as well choose to stay at the Sheraton Hotel. I believe you will fall in love with everything here like me.

The hot spring starts at two o'clock in the afternoon. There is a shuttle bus in front of the hotel that goes directly to the hot spring. You can bring your own hotel bathrobe. After all, it is a bit cold when you come out of the water. If you don't bring it, you can rent it there for 20 yuan, and the bath towel is free. There are about a dozen kinds of hot springs indoors, as well as a paddling pool. Drinking water is provided for free. You don‚Äôt need to bring it yourself. There are basic equipment such as a hair dryer, and you can dry your swimsuit. After soaking in the hot springs, you can go back to the hotel to rest and have dinner.

During the stay, you can contact her for anything. The attitude is very good, very professional. I booked a room facing the Moon Square, with large windows on both sides and a large balcony. The scenery outside the window is beautiful, and there is a light show at night. The room is big, well-equipped and very sanitary. The carpet is old, but it is very clean. The Chinese restaurant on the third floor of the hotel is also delicious. This experience was really good, and I will come again next time I have the opportunity.

The lake view room on the 11th floor where we lived has a large terrace (should be the essence) and has a wide field of vision. In the distance where the lake and sky are the same color, there is a long merchant ship (should be a shipping route), which has been rising As far as the eye can see, a vivid picture is displayed; nearby are the trails along the lake and some businesses, which are dazzling under the lights at night, and you can even hear the sound of the lake lapping the river bank, as if you are at the seaside.
    The room is not very big, but it is enough to live in. After nine years of operation, it is just at the stage of neither new nor old. The bathroom part may take up two-fifths of the space, the huge round bathtub and the texture of the sanitary ware all indicate the grade, and the jade paved floor and countertops are quite exotic (though I personally don't like dazzling a feeling of). Open for business; I was the only one to enjoy the swimming pool, and the security guard was not absent throughout the whole process; only two employees of the SPA were sticking to their posts, but they also provided service (although the level of professionalism was lower than my expectations); although the buffet dinner was only 2, 30 The dishes are still quite rich, and the small Filipino band is also performing diligently; the night light show is staged as usual, and there is no hasty ending, think about the energy consumption...
